Since `sin(v)` is linearly independent from any polynomial in v (like `v`, `v³`), and `v*sin(x)` is linearly independent from `v*x²` or other polynomial products, **no candidate can match the GT**.

Let me verify: Could `v + v³` approximate `sin(v)` exactly? No - `sin(v) = v - v³/6 + v⁵/120 - ...` is an infinite series, not a finite polynomial. Exact equivalence is impossible.

Similarly, `v*sin(x)` cannot be represented by `v*x²` or any polynomial in x times v.
